###Martell History###

#Maron and Myriah have been put in, Daenerys has been made and connected to Nearys and Aegon the Unworthy plus Olyvar. Martells now have Targ blood. :)
#I've put an equal number of female and male martells rulers. To simulate the absolute-cognatic succession.
#The first few would be Emperor tier Prince titles for the histories too. Until Maron, who'd be bumped down to King tier Prince.
###############################
###Unbowed, Unbent, Unbroken###
###############################

####Dornish Princes and Princesses since Aegon's Landing
22001 = {
	name="Hodor"	# Emperor title Princess in the family histories. # Note all legacy Martell's have been given good traits because... they kept a kingdom independent from the Dragons for 160 years. If they were idiots, Aegon would have conquered them and if not him Daeron or Reach and Storm Lords in days gone by. They need some respect :-)
	female=yes
	dynasty=1
	
	dna = ravamnuijhx
	properties = db0cja000000
	
	martial=11 # stopped Aegon the Conqueror after the Yellow toad refused Rhaenys offer to bend the knee.
	diplomacy=10 # Kept Dorne's independence.
	intrigue=6
	stewardship=4
	learning=11  # learned the mistakes of King Mern and Loren of the Rock and Reach.
	
	religion="the_seven"
	culture="salt_dornish"
	
	add_trait="genius"
	
	father=6083001
	mother=4083001

	7920.1.1 = {
		birth="7920.1.1"  #80yo at time of Aegon's Landing in 7998.
		effect = { health = 5 }
	} 
	7934.1.1={add_trait="brilliant_strategist"}
	7936.1.1 = {
		add_matrilineal_spouse = 42001
	}
	7938.1.1={add_trait="diligent"
	          add_trait="brave"
	          add_trait="deceitful" 
			  add_trait="gluttonous"
	          add_trait="patient"}
